3. The gift items written on Ctrip are false propaganda. Some gift items have been told that they are not open when they arrive at the place. Think Want to play with the whole family? Spend your own money. We called the hotel to ask about it. At the beginning, we confirmed with us that both the big and the small can play, but later they said that the policy has been changed and we need to pay for it at our own expense. In the process of making a call, A answered the phone, and if he could not answer the question, he transferred it to B, and B transferred it to C. It seems that their tactic is, if they annoy the customer, they don't ask, and there is no problem. Really superb service skills.
4. The breakfast buffet is rich in styles but there are almost no meat dishes, only eggs and flour sausages are barely considered meat dishes, but compared with the front desk, this is nothing.
